\index{mmf\_msess.h@{mmf\_msess.h}!Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp@{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp}}
\index{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp@{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp}!mmf\_msess.h@{mmf\_msess.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp()}{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigIdPartp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mmf\+\_\+\+M\+Sess\+Get\+Orig\+Id\+Partp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Name,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Uri }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get original identity of participant U\+RI from message session. 

The participant is the session initiator who initialized this message session. It will return local U\+RI if local client is the session initiator. It will return identity uri if session invitation has P-\/\+Asserted-\/\+Identity information.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Name} & The participant name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The participant U\+RI.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
ppc\+Name and ppc\+Uri should be freed by Zos\+\_\+\+Sys\+Str\+Free.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & Get original participant successfully. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & Get original participant failed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{mmf__msess_8h_a467bfe6ff5d2d21814ef8f08be3a97b2}\label{mmf__msess_8h_a467bfe6ff5d2d21814ef8f08be3a97b2}} 
\index{mmf\_msess.h@{mmf\_msess.h}!Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp@{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp}}
\index{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp@{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp}!mmf\_msess.h@{mmf\_msess.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp()}{Mmf\_MSessGetOrigPartp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+I\+NT Mmf\+\_\+\+M\+Sess\+Get\+Orig\+Partp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+U\+I\+NT}]{i\+Sess\+Id,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Name,  }\item[{Z\+C\+H\+AR $\ast$$\ast$}]{ppc\+Uri }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



M\+MF Get original paticipant from message session. 

The paticipant is the session initiator who initialized this message session. It will return local uri if local client is the session initiator.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Name} & The participant name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ppc\+Uri} & The participant uri.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
ppc\+Name and ppc\+Uri should be freed by Zos\+\_\+\+Sys\+Str\+Free.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Z\+OK} & Get original paticipant successfully. \\
\hline
{\em Z\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED} & Get original paticipant failed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

M\+MF Send geolocation through session. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Sess\+Id} & The session id. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em z\+Cookie} & The user cookie. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+G\+Info\+Type} & geo info type, see@\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+G\+F\+\_\+\+G\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Free\+Text} & The free text. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em d\+Latitude} & The latitude of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em d\+Longitude} & The longitude of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em f\+Radius} & The radius of user place. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pc\+Label} & The label string, if Z\+N\+U\+LL indicate user\textquotesingle{}s own position, else other position. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em i\+Msg\+Type} & The message type, see E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+M\+F\+\_\+\+M\+S\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pi\+Msg\+Id} & The id for geolocation message.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Note\+: if radius value is equal to 0, the coordinate is a point, if radius value is bigger than 0, the coordinate is a circle.

{\em Z\+OK} & Sending successfully. \\
\hline
